\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{integral_8h_source_l01231}01231 \textcolor{comment}{  /// 3D Gaussian integration class for tets.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{integral_8h_source_l01232}01232 \textcolor{comment}{  /// 45 integration points. This integration scheme can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{integral_8h_source_l01233}01233 \textcolor{comment}{  /// integrate up to eighth-\/order polynomials exactly and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{integral_8h_source_l01234}01234 \textcolor{comment}{  /// is therefore a suitable "{}full"{} integration scheme}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{integral_8h_source_l01235}01235 \textcolor{comment}{  /// for quartic elements in which the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{integral_8h_source_l01236}01236 \textcolor{comment}{  /// highest-\/order polynomial is fourth order.}}
